< Review>
This restaurant  is newly remodeled.  Has a nice bar and big flat screens for watching sports. They  have a great top shelf liquor  selection as well as a good selection if tap and bottled beers. Lets get down to  the food......
I ordered the steak burrito  smothered  with red sauce and  cheese which included beans and rice. Everything was fresh and had good flavor. Chips were fresh and warm,  salsa fresh and had a little  kick but not to spicy,  it was also very good and couldn't  stop dipping! The ambiance was quite enjoyable, and the staff is friendly. Great for  a dinner date,  work lunch or  for a family  night. Over all one of  the  best Mexican restaurants in Tracy, Great I know  because  I've been  trying  them all out!  There portions are enormous so be prepared to  take home a doggy bag.  I was surprised I couldn't  finish my meal. Why are you  still reading this?  you should be driving to Sonia's!!!</Review>

< Text>
Me and my boyfriend are both vegan as well as new to Tracy, and we try not to cause too much trouble when we order in places that aren't conventionally vegan. Unknown to me and him the owner and chef, Jordan, goes vegan for lent and she personally came out to make sure she got our order correct, even if it wasn't necessarily on the menu, she also brought us an appetizer that she made vegan for us on the house. I can't begin to describe the amount of respect I have gained for this place, not to mention the food was tasty, fresh and the homemade guacamole/salsa is delicious! Excellent customer service, great tasting food, and really nice environment. Definitely recommend.< /Text>

5< /Rating>
<Review>Just moved to Tracy yesterday, and this is the first restaurant we've tried for Mexican. Being from the central valley, I have a certain flavor and style of Mexican fare that I prefer, and Sonia's hit them all perfectly! I've had Mexican all over the US and Europe, and I can never find this quality. They may call it Pueblo food, but it's my favorite.

1st- The amazing bartender made the BEST Cadillac margaritas I've had in years. PERFECT. The service was FANTASTIC ALL AROUND, and we even got a chance to thank the chef.

2nd- True test one= perfectly seasoned and cooked rice and beans. Must've been homemade, nothing from a can tastes that amazing.

3rd- True test two= I always order a chile relleno to judge the quality of a restaurant. I can't say enough things about this. The sauce was phenomenal and done correctly, I like the added addition of peas. The chile was cooked right, and stuffed with cheese but not overwhelmingly. Egg batter was spot on.

4th- Normally I do not like carrots in my ground beef. I didn't even NOTICE THEY WERE THERE in my enchilada. It was so good, I couldn't have cared less, and actually finally understood the reasoning of flavor mix after having it here.

5th- PORTIONS. Had we been able to stop eating, we would have had a lot of leftovers! My husband ordered the Cancun Platter. Unless you have two stomachs, order with caution! However, my skinny husband ATE THE ENTIRE PLATE.

So, if you enjoy food from the central valley, you will adore this place. And even then, try it anyway because it is worth it. We will be going back for dinner this week! They even have daily specials, tv's, fun Taco Thursdays where they make homemade tortillas and you make your own tacos. I can't WAIT!!!

Thank you Sonia's, you are FABULOUS.</Review>< Pics>

This review is specifically for Manon, although I'm sure the rest of the staff is also great. We called to schedule an in-person self-guided tour one morning with someone else (didn't catch their name) and Manon called a couple hours later to follow up. It's a pleasure to have you as members of the Regency Palms community and know that our mission is to make this a place that you are proud to call home.\n\nIf there is anything you need, always feel free to reach out to us!\n\nThanks again!"}<//resp>< Text>
While no management company can predict how a tenant will be 100%, the current staff here has done a great job of assuring that we have great neighbors with respect for the community and for others who share their space.  The occasional bad neighbor is always something that happens when you are apartment living, but the RP team seems to have managed to keep that to a minimum.

They have a great Maint staff that does all they can to keep a very aging property, vibrant and alive with quick turnarounds on reported issues and pretty solid grounds keeping in general.  RP may not have all the most modern amenities in the units, but they are by no means falling apart or in bad repair.  I constantly see the staff here working to improve the property and maintain it while still offering a fairly reasonable (for a beach city in Southern California) rent rate.

The staff is friendly and go out of their way to know their residents, especially those who go out of their way to help build those relationships.  You cannot force people to be open and understanding, but the demeanor of the staff here, enables those who choose to have those connections with staff, are enabled to do so.

My wife an I have happily lived here for almost 6 years now, in several units, 1 and 2 bdrm, and have been very happy since day one, but never more than we are with the current staff!

No apartment complex is perfect and nowhere will ever have 100% satisfaction with all of our neighbors, there are just too many personalities in the world for that, but RP does a pretty good job of building a friendly and safe community for it's residents...with very few exceptions in our experience!

Gill<//Text>

My sincere request:  PLEASE INCREASE YOUR STAFF.</review>

<user>107928880714624295405</user><GmapID>0x80dd267d9171e71f:0x4629ff8ede4674b0<//GmapID>< Review>
We absolutely love our new apartment in the Regency Palms Apartment community. We had our reservations at first, concerned about living alongside so many others in this 310 unit complex. We were assured that we would be happy, but if for any reason we decided it wasn't going to workout for us, we were given a 30-day satisfaction period from our move in date to change to another available unit OR to move out, No Harm No Foul, should we decide. Well, needless to say, we are VERY happy and wish to stay for a very long time
.
This IS a dog friendly community, but we ourselves are NOT dog owners. Regardless, they are no bother, but instead a joy to watch...and play with when the opportunity arises. There are green belts all through the complex so whether it's to walk your dog or just for taking an evening stroll with your loved ones, the grounds here at the Regency Palms have beautiful , well-kept landscaping and big beautiful trees to offer shade on those hot summer days. There are Doggy Waste Stations strategically placed all through the complex to help keep the grassy areas as clean and sanitary as possible. I see the Orkin man here every week inspecting and treating all areas and issues that may cause a problem if gone unattended. Due to there diligent and professional work, this community is bug free. I haven't seen one critter in over 2-months.

The Leasing Office Staff, including their maintenance and cleaning crews, have been an absolute blast to deal with. I've had a service request or two that I needed assistance with. Once reported to the Leasing Team, our issues were quickly and efficiently dealt with keeping me a happy & content camper :) Their five (5) laundry room facilities are always clean and available. The washers are bigger and less expensive than the Laundromat across the street in the shopping center. Trust me, we've checked. And speaking of local shopping & recreation, the Regency Palms is located within walking distance from grocery stores, Home Depot and lots of other much needed services. Very convenient! It's a miles walk to the Library, Central Park, AND Goldenwest College, and not to forget the Westminster Mall.
I have made some good friends already and all the people who live here are very nice. One of my favorite things to do here on a hot day is to go lay out, get wet and socialize poolside, in any one of their 3-well maintained pools + Jacuzzi. When I'm out enjoying the pool area, It's just like being at a Palm Springs resort.

In closing, let me just say this.........."If you are looking for a great place to live and  haven't checked out The Regency Palms yet, What Are You Waiting For?" Call and set up an appointment for a tour by one of their fantastic Leasing Agents. I promise , You WON'T be let down! :)))</Review>

< review>
My new wing spot in North Hollywood!  Free parking in the back.  I was blown away by this place. Not only was the food hot and fresh, it took less than eight minutes.  Granted all I ordered was a ten piece hot wing and curly fries, but I've waiting over 20 minutes before at other wing places in the area.  The night I went, they were also pretty busy with a lot of carry out orders.  The dinning area has a big screen TV in the dining area so I decided to stay and watch one of the football games that happen to be on.  If you want to get rowdy and drink while watching a game, I would still recommend Big Wangs, but that's the ONLY reason.  House of Wings is superior in every way from the food to the service.   The ranch they served with my wings was also amazing, according to the guy behind the counter, it's homemade, made fresh daily.<//review>

<Text>I was looking into upgrading my OEM exhaust because it didn't have that sporty sound note that I was looking for.  My local muffler shop who I've gone with in the past was asking for too much (x2) to have my aftermarket exhaust installed so I needed to look elsewhere.  A few weeks prior to deciding to upgrade to an aftermarket exhaust, I was having the vehicle smog-checked.  Luckily my smog test guy and friend for many years referred me to his friend Andy here at Classic Muffler Service Center.  I gave Andy a call and he scheduled some time the following Saturday to have my aftermarket exhaust installed.  I didn't have the convenience of driving a few miles away to my old shop, but the 20 minute drive down from my town to Andy's shop was well worth it.

Andy charged me 1/2 of what my old muffler shop wanted and the results are outstanding.  Not only was the new aftermarket exhaust installed perfectly but it was done in about 45 minutes.  During the entire time, Andy and I bonded and had a great conversation while he was installing my new exhaust system.  His shop is clean and well organized, but the entire business complex is filled with cars that are visiting other shops and/or ones that are in the queue to be worked on, so finding a parking spot can be a challenge.

Now back to the install, another customer was there to fill-in the conversation and the entire experience was a blast!  I mentioned to Andy that I had another person who was interested in buying my OEM exhaust and he was surprised that I didn't want to throw it away, so I asked him to cut the exhaust into 3 sections (some at the existing weld-points) and he did so per my request.  Good thing I was able to resell that OEM exhaust the same day, and the guy I sold it to had Andy install it in his ride.  So in return, I was able to bring Andy some more business.

Not only was I super-happy with the installation, including the price I paid and also the friendly conversation I had with Andy and the other customer, I left with a big grin on my face once I got back onto the main road, hit the accelerator and finally let the exhaust rip.  My car now has the sound I've been looking for thanks to Andy.

Since Andy's shop is so popular, I might add that I did have to wait for about 1hr since another customer had already had an earlier time slot before mine.  While I waited in my car, a few other customers came by for quick fixes and after Andy helped out one customer, he didn't take any payment, even after the customer insisted.  Andy just said, "Next time, don't worry about it!".  Andy is such a friendly guy, but he's also generous and understanding.  He's more concerned about his customers and providing them solutions rather than just taking their money.  I noticed that he does take-in everyone who visits his shop and that's probably the reason why he has so many great reviews.

If you're waiting for your turn, have patience and don't feel like others cut in front of you, because Andy doesn't forget that you're next in line.  I initially had that feeling while waiting for my turn, but I quickly realized that if Andy knows that if the customer needs a quick fix, he'll quickly help them out before sending them off on their merry way.  No reason at all that I should knock-off a star for that.  It's just the nature of his business.  Ultimately everyone gets serviced, just need to be patient.  Afterall, I did show-up there to his shop on a Saturday morning.<//Text>< user_id>

< Review>
Everything about Livermore Optometry visits is good.  Ease of making an appointment. Professional, friendly and competent staff. Although I haven't done much shopping around their prices seem competitive.  However, they, and so many other medical offices (dentists, etc) now want to take up too much of my time answering "thank you" e mails and taking surveys.  I took the survey, but that wasn't enough.  I immediately got a 'please leave a remark' request even though I had ignored the request at the end of the survey.  So my ONLY complaint is too much soliciting of opinions.  If they had an opt out of the survey or comments, I would definitely take it.<//Review>
